***betichten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:betichten.html>betichten</a> (65901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly formed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beticht.html>beticht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">legal claim, accusation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. However, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beticht.html>beticht</a></i> does not appear to be attested in modern Dutch (after 1500) whereas the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:betichten.html>betichten</a></i> only appears around that time. Since it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unlikely that a verb would be formed from a noun that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> falling out of use already, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> likely that it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> formed directly as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ticht</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i> instead.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:betichten.html>betichten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to accuse falsely</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">betichting</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:betichten.html>betichten</a></b>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:betogen.html>betogen</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:toog.html>togen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">tōgen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ataugijaną</i>, a derivation of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*augijaną</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*augô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">eye</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oog.html>oog</a></i>).

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:betonen.html>betonen</a></i>. ***betoog.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:betoog.html>betoog</a> (25029)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">betooch</i>. Equivalent to a deverbal neutrum from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:betogen.html>betogen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:betoog.html>betoog</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:betogen.html>betogen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:betoog.html>betoogje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>argument, plea <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">subjective discourse in which one argues in favour of something</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> proof, evidence</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> demonstration, act of showing</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.

***betrachten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:betrachten.html>betrachten</a> (77089)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:betrachten.html>betrachten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to look at, to observe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bitrahton</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trachten.html>trachten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:betrachten.html>betrachten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to exercise or consider carefully</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <span class="Latn" lang="en">pursue</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nastreven.html>nastreven</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">beogen</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The verb in the meaning "to exercise carefully" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> limited to a number of expressions, like:
</p>
<ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plicht.html>plicht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:betrachten.html>betrachten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> acquit oneself of one's duty</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nodige.html>nodige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zorgvuldigheid.html>zorgvuldigheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:betrachten.html>betrachten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> exercise due care</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">betrachting</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:betrachten.html>betrachten</a></b>

***betrappen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:betrappen.html>betrappen</a> (8837)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Alongside older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">betrapen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">betrapen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to catch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trappen.html>trappen</a></i>, with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trappen.html>trappen</a></i> in the now-obsolete sense "catch, <a href = vnd.unilang:trap.html>trap</a>". The reason for the single consonant and long vowel in Middle Dutch <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unclear.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take by surprise, to catch unaware, someone who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> doing something they should not be</li></ol>

***betreden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:betreden.html>betreden</a> (7220)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:betreden.html>betreden</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:treden.html>treden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:betreden.html>betreden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tread upon</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to enter, to come in</li></ol>

***betweter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:betweter.html>betweter</a> (21124)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ca. 1600, from obsolete <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bet <a href = vnd.unilang:weten.html>weten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know better</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>, thus “better-knower”, one who always knows it better. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">Bet</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the adverbial form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beter.html>beter</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">better</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Besserwisser</i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:betwisten.html>betwisten</a></i>. ***beuk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beuk.html>beuk</a> (15201)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From eastern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bo.html>boke</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:boeken.html>boeke</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*buoka</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*bōkijā</i>. Western varieties of Dutch, including generally Standard Dutch, do not have <a href = vnd.unilang:umlaut.html>umlaut</a> of long vowels. The eastern variety with <a href = vnd.unilang:umlaut.html>umlaut</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> probably adopted to avoid homonymy with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>boek</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beuk.html>beuk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beuken.html>beuken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beuk.html>beukje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A beech, tree of the genus <i>Fagus</i>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">beukenboom</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>The common beech, <i>Fagus sylvatica</i>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gewone.html>gewone</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beuk.html>beuk</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">beukenboom</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beul.html>beul</a> (8528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">buel</i>, earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">buedel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*budil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*budilaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beul.html>beul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beulen.html>beulen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beul.html>beultje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An executioner, torturer, one who <a href = vnd.unilang:carries.html>carries</a> out executions and other judicial corporal punishments
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scherprechter.html>scherprechter</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cruel person, in act or sadistic streak
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sadist.html>sadist</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">wreedaard</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***beunhaas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beunhaas.html>beunhaas</a> (109010)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">beun</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">attic</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haas.html>haas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hare.html>hare</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Böhnhase</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">bönhase</i>, originally meaning “cat”. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bönhase</i> for more.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beunhaas.html>beunhaas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beunhazen.html>beunhazen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beunhaas.html>beunhaasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tradesman or merchant, especially a tailor, who wasn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> associated with a guild
<ul><li><b>1843</b>, C. A. den <a href = vnd.unilang:tex.html>Tex</a> amp; J. <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Hall,<i>Regtsgeleerd bijblad</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. V, 19.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beurs.html>beurs</a> (3622)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">borse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">bourse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bursa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βύρσα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">búrsa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beurs.html>beurs</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beurzen.html>beurzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beurs.html>beursje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>purse, both as object and treasury</li>
<li>bursary</li>
<li>scholarship</li>
<li>stock exchange</li>
<li>event or place where goods are exchanged; a trade fair</li></ol>

***beurt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beurt.html>beurt</a> (1574)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">boerte</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beuren.html>beuren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beurt.html>beurt</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beurten.html>beurten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beurtje.html>beurtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>turn (a chance to use (something) shared in sequence with others)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>Wie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beurt.html>beurt</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Whose <b>turn</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> it?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>uw</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beurt.html>beurt</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It's your <b>turn</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vehicles</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> maintenance, service

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bevel.html>bevel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">command</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to have</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>. First known attestations from ca. 1535 and thus perhaps after <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Befehl(s)haber</i> (1490), probably already <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">bevelhaber</i> (1335, copy 16th c.).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beven.html>beven</a> (10164)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bēven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bivon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bibāną</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bever.html>bever</a> (11516)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bēver</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bevar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bebruz</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bevinden.html>bevinden</a> (6097)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bevinden.html>bevinden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bifindan</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vinden.html>vinden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to discover, to find</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be located, to find oneself
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>Onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bevindt.html>bevindt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vloeibaar.html>vloeibare</a> buitenkern (<a href = vnd.unilang:waarin.html>waarin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> aardmagnetisch <a href = vnd.unilang:veld.html>veld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opgewekt.html>opgewekt</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaste.html>vaste</a> binnenkern.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Under the <a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a> <b>are located</b> a fluid outer core (in which the Earth's magnetic field <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> generated) and a fixed inner core.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***bevlekken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bevlekken.html>bevlekken</a> (77072)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bevlecken</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vlekken.html>vlekken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bevlekken.html>bevlekken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stain, to soil</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to masturbate, to self-pollute</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bevlekking</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">zelfbevlekking</span></li></ul>
